WinInteropUtils
Table of Contents

Enum HRESULT

Namespace
FireBlade.WinInteropUtils
Assembly
WinInteropUtils.dll

Defines common HRESULT values. Values starting with S_ indicate success, while those starting with E_ indicate an error.

public enum HRESULT
Extension Methods
EnumExtensions.GetValues(Enum)
